   "idaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī madramabhū"dityādi "namo devebhya" ityanto nigadarūpo	"idam dyAvApRTivI madram-aBU"t-ityAdi "namaH deveBya" iti-antaH nigada-rUpaH-
   mantraḥ sūktavākastasyaca sūktavākatvamagre vyaktīkariṣyate /	mantraH sUktavAkaH-tasya-ca sUktavAka-tvam-agre vyaktIkarizyate /
   tena mantreṇa prastaraṃ darbhamuṣṭimagnau prakṣipatīti vākyasyārthaḥ //	tena mantreNa prastaram darBa-muzwim-agnO prakzipati-iti vAkyasya-arTaH //
   tatra gauṇasāmarthyasya śrutisahāyatayā viniyojakatve 'bhihite	tatra gONa-sAmarTyasya Sruti-sahAya-tayA viniyojaka-tve aBihite
   mukhyasāmarthyasyāpi tatsahāyatānirūpaṇena pūrvoktasya	muKya-sAmarTyasya-api tad-sahAya-tA-nirUpaNena pUrva-uktasya

   kālopalakṣaṇatayānvayena kālārthaḥ saṃbandhaḥ hotrāsminmantre paṭhyamāne	kAla-upalakzaNa-tayA-anvayena kAla-arTaH saMbanDaH hotrA-asmin-mantre paWyamAne
   tatpāṭhakāle prastaraṃ praharediti, athavā sūktavākasya karaṇatayānvayena	tad-pAWa-kAle prastaram praharet-iti, aTavA sUktavAkasya karaNa-tayA-anvayena
   praharaṇāṅgamiti saṃśayaṃ ca spaṣṭatvādanuktvā pūrvapakṣamevāha --------	praharaNa-aFgam-iti saMSayam ca spazwa-tvAt-anuktvA pUrva-pakzam-eva-Aha --------
   tatreti //	tatra-iti //
   iṣṭadevateti //	izwadevatA-iti //
   ājyabhāgānūyājānteṣu karmasūddiṣṭā agnyādayo devatā ityarthaḥ /	Ajya-BAga-anUyA-jAntezu karmasu-uddizwAH agni-AdayaH devatAH iti-arTaH /
   upayukteti //	upayuktA-iti //
   "prastarejuhūmāsādayati sarvā vā struca" iti vākyena strugdhāraṇe	"prastarejuhUma-AsAdayati sarvAH vA struca" iti vAkyena stru-c-DAraNe
   upayuktaprastarapratipattitvenetyarthaḥ /	upayukta-prastara-pratipatti-tvena-iti-arTaH /
   kṛtārthatvameva hyākāṅkṣāvirahasaṃpādanenāṅgāṅgisaṃbandhavighaṭaka-	kRtArTa-tvam-eva hi-AkAFkzA-viraha-saMpAdanena-aFga-aFgi-saMbanDa-viGawaka-
   mityatastameva sūtropāttatayā hetumāha ------- kṛtārthatvāditi //	miti-atas-tam-eva sUtra-upAttatayA hetum-Aha ------ kRtArTa-tvAt-iti //
   evañca cāturthikanyāyena kālārthasaṃbandhaṃ dṛṣṭāntavyājena sādhayati	evaQca cAturTika-nyAyena kAla-arTa-saMbanDam dRzwAnta-vyAjena sADayati
   -------- darśapūrṇamāsābhyāmiti //	------- darSa-pUrNamAsAByAm-iti //
   yadyapyatra dṛṣṭānta iva kālārthasaṃbandhabodhakaḥ ktvāpratyayo nāsti;	yadi-api-atra dRzwAntaH iva kAla-arTa-saMbanDa-boDakaH ktvA-apratyayaH nAsti;
   tathāpi kṛtārthataiva pūrvoktarītyā kālārthatāpādane hetuḥ,	taTA-api kRtArTa-tA-eva pUrva-ukta-rItyA kAla-arTa-tA-ApAdane hetuH,
   ktvāpratyayastu kālaviśeṣe paurvāparyarūpe niyāmakamātramiti na doṣaḥ /	ktvA-apratyayaH-tu kAla-viSeze pOrvAparya-rUpe niyAmaka-mAtram-iti na dozaH /
   kathaṃ tarhi karaṇatvaparatṛtīyopapattirityata āha -------- tṛtīyā ceti /	kaTam tarhi karaNa-tva-paratRtIyA-upapattiH-iti-atas Aha ------- tRtIyA ca-iti /
   "itthaṃbhūtalakṣaṇe tṛtīye" tyanuśāsanena gamakatvarūpalakṣaṇārthatvena	"itTaMBUta-lakzaNe tRtIye" tyanuSAsanena gamaka-tva-rUpa-lakzaNa-arTa-tvena
   sūktavākavṛttigamakatvābhidhānāttasyaca tatkālīnatvasaṃpādanena	sUktavAka-vRtti-gamaka-tva-aBiDAnAt-tasya-ca tad-kAlIna-tva-saMpAdanena
   saṃbhavāttṛtīyopapattirityarthaḥ //	saMBavAt-tRtIya-upapattiH-iti-arTaH //

   etena ------- yat jñānajanakatvarūpalakṣaṇatvābhidhānenaiva jñānakriyāyā	etena ------ yat jQAna-janaka-tva-rUpa-lakzaNa-tva-aBiDAnena-eva jQAna-kriyAyAH-

   svajanyabhāvanājñānaviṣayatāsaṃbandhena	sva-janya-BAvanA-jQAna-vizaya-tA-saMbanDena

   evañca pūrvoktapraiṣamantravadiha prakaraṇe mantrasyānvayānupapatterna	evaQca pUrva-ukta-prEza-mantra-vat-iha prakaraNe mantrasya-anvaya-anupapatteH-na
   tadaṅgatvaṃ mantrasya, nahi "idaṃ havirajuṣatāvīvṛdhata maho jyāyo	tad-aFga-tvam mantrasya, na-hi "idam haviH-ajuzatA-avIvRData mahaH jyAyo
   'kṛte"ti mantrabhāgasya puroḍāśasevayā vṛddho 'gniḥ svasminyajamāne	akRte"ti mantra-BAgasya puroxASa-sevayA vRdDaH agniH svasmin-yajamAne
   tejobāhulyaṃ kṛtavānityarthaḥ praharaṇe saṃbhavati;	tejaH-bAhulyam kRtavAn-iti-arTaH praharaNe saMBavati;
   bhūtanirdeśānupapatteḥ, pratipatteḥ devatānapekṣaṇācca, ataḥ kālārthaḥ	BUta-nirdeSa-anupapatteH, pratipatteH devatA-anapekzaNAt-ca, atas kAla-arTaH
   saṃbandha ityabhipretya pūrvapakṣamupasaṃharati --------- ataśceti //	saMbanDaH iti-aBipretya pUrva-pakzam-upasaMharati -------- atas-ca-iti //
   prastarapraharaṇasya barhiṣi prastarasādanānantaraṃ	prastara-praharaNasya barhizi prastara-sAdana-anantaram

   puroḍāśādiviṣayatve 'pyagnyādiḥ puroḍāśādi sevitavān tena vṛddho	puroxASa-Adi-vizaya-tve api-agni-AdiH puroxASa-Adi sevitavAn tena vRdDaH-
